		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/uuid_utils.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/uuid_utils.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php') !== '31e57ab1252e66122b9c66ff0434a644fb23076e') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php') !== '1e536905501c72a36626831b57f9bd18266b1387') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/uuid_utils.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php') !== '31e57ab1252e66122b9c66ff0434a644fb23076e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/uuid_utils.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'bf561d1146bd426403e743a6af8f88ba5cec33cb') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'bf561d1146bd426403e743a6af8f88ba5cec33cb') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'b2e6f6f5aa61fa296dfcb85531ed3a65d431d2e2') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'bf561d1146bd426403e743a6af8f88ba5cec33cb') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}
